                      <div data-reactid="324">
                       With private entrance and garden access, this artistic and soulful abode will provide the peace &amp; comfort of a bygone time. On a quiet tree lined street, one may walk to the beach or to nearby cafes and restaurants to enjoy the flavor of the Santa Monica experience. Coffee/Tea provided.

                      <div data-reactid="325">
                       The 'Enchanted Garden Suite' is a secret retreat in the heart of Santa Monica. Your private entrance to a peaceful, bygone era, is a time worn, wooden gate, decorated with old tin Milagros. Step into a flourishing, tangle of garden with gurgling fountain, behind a restored 1912 Craftsman to find your cozy bedroom &amp; bath. Your room is artistically and lovingly appointed with eclectic folk art treasures from our world travels. At the foot of your Queen size rattan bed is a lovely 1920's faux fireplace. Your bathroom has fluffy cotton towels, a pedestal sink and tiled shower. In the evening, original pewter and brass light fixtures cast a warm, candle-like glow. Flanking the bed are stacks of wicker and metal vintage travel suitcases, with antique table lamps for your reading pleasure and a 40" flat screen TV sits on the fireplace mantle with a DVD player. From a quiet, tree lined street, the beach, is an easy 14 minute walk. You can also stroll to popular, nearby cafes, restaurants and shops and experience why Santa Monica is one of the worlds most popular destinations. Sit and relax at our artistic rock and mosaic table in the garden, enjoying your morning tea and coffee that is provided while hopefully witnessing the joy of colorful hummingbirds and finches bathing in the nearby garden fountain. We look forward to making your stay in 'The Enchanted Garden Suite' a memorable one.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="326">
                       Our home is in a quiet tree lined residential area within a 15 minute walk to the beach, food markets, interesting restaurants, and public transportation.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="327">
                       <li data-reactid="328"><p data-reactid="329">I was asked to fly out to LA from Texas very last minute for a job interview, so you could say I was a bit manic. Thankfully, I found Kathy and Bob's place. Close to the beach and very private. I loved sitting in the courtyard and leaving the room door open to hear the trickling of the bird fountain. The bedroom's warm and eclectic aesthetic really put my mind at ease and felt very home-y. I appreciated all the interesting art and quirky little knick-knacks. The bathroom was clean and updated. Shower pressure was fantastic (especially after long days of walking). I was working most of my stay, so I didn't speak to Kathy and Bob very much. BUT they were very communicative and made it clear that I could come to them if I needed anything. I may be returning to LA very soon and would definitely stay here again! </p><span data-reactid="330">Jessica</span><span data-reactid="331">2014-07-27T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                       <li data-reactid="332"><p data-reactid="333">Our stay at Kathy and Bob's was very nice. The separate entrance is great for privacy and independence. The room was clean and comfortable and we had our own mini-fridge as well as Direct TV in the room. We would definitely stay here again!</p><span data-reactid="334">Elliot</span><span data-reactid="335">2015-08-23T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                      <div data-reactid="953">
                       You can't beat the location of this cute and cozy studio with private patio and free parking. Clean, uncluttered, smoke &amp; pet free and fully equipped, this ground floor unit has terracotta tile floors, a quality queen size bed and free wifi. Close to Rose Ave (1 block) and the famous Venice Boardwalk &amp; Beach (10 minute walk), Abbot Kinney, Venice Canals, Main Street, Santa Monica Pier and 4th Street Promenade.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="954">
                       LOCATION, LOCATION, LOCATION! This is why the biggest and hippest online companies on the planet have chosen to put their newest offices just down the road! The best thing about the studio is that it is superbly situated only blocks away from the trendy Rose Ave, the beach, Abbot Kinney Blvd., Whole Foods and Santa Monica's sophisticated Main Street. It is close to all the best shopping, beach and nightlife yet located on a quiet and safe residential street full of trees. We suggest getting on a beach cruiser to explore the Venice Canals, Venice Beach and Santa Monica. If your up to it the bike path will take you to Manhattan Beach, Hermosa Beach or Redondo Beach as well. There is also a "Breeze Bikes" station two blocks away; a very convenient grab-and-go bicycle vending station. If you want to experience the funkier side of Venice Beach explore the Venice Beach Boardwalk. Street performers, artists, musicians, muscle beach, skateboard park, surfing, volleyball, it's all a short 10 min walk. The Santa Monica Pier, Santa Monica Aquarium and Santa Monica 4th Street Promenade and Mall are 2 miles away, easy to walk, drive, bike or Uber. As most beach properties along the California Coastline, this property is not equipped with an A/C unit. With average beach temperatures ranging from 65 to 75 degrees year round, air conditioning is not generally needed in our beach areas. For our warmer days open windows to allow the fresh ocean air to circulate and cool the property.
                      </div>

                      <div data-reactid="1430">
                       Room w/ private staircase, closet and bathroom in brand new, architectural home in Venice. Three blocks from Abbott Kinney and another three blocks to the beach. Enjoy a luxurious home base while exploring Venice and LA!
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1431">
                       Luxurious, spacious private room with its own private staircase, bathroom and closet. There is no door at the top of the staircase but the staircase is in a separate wing of the house - no one other than you has access to the staircase. The room is in a brand new, private single family home West of Lincoln in the heart of Venice. High speed wifi and morning coffee included. West of Lincoln, East of Abbott Kinney on Milwood Ave -- the nicest street in Venice! The house is three blocks to Abbott Kinney and three more blocks to the beach. 15 minute drive to LAX. 3 minute walk to Ralphs (supermarket) and CVS (drug store) on Lincoln Blvd and 15 minute walk to Whole Foods / Rose Ave. restaurants. Gjelina, Salt Air, Tasting Kitchen and other Abbott Kinney restaurants and shops are a 10-15 minute walk. There are two hypoallergenic 10 lb dogs that live in the house. They are well-behaved, don't shed and won't have access to your room as long as you close the door.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1432">
                       In the heart of Venice, west of Lincoln. The area is safe and has a great beach community vibe. The street the house is on is wide and lined with palm trees. Steps from Lincoln and very close to Abbott Kinney and the beach.
